<script>
try {
  function auidCookie() {
    return document.cookie.split('; ').find((c)=>c.startsWith('auid='))?.slice(5) ?? null;
}
  function clientFlagrRequestUri(ctx) {
    const entityIdQuery = `entityId=${ctx.auid ? encodeURIComponent(ctx.auid) : null}`;
    const flagTagQuery = `flagTag=salo-web`;
    const segmentationParametersQuery = Object.entries(ctx).map(([k, v])=>`${k}=${encodeURIComponent(JSON.stringify(v))}`).join('&');
    const featureFlagEvaluationQuery = `${entityIdQuery}&${flagTagQuery}&${segmentationParametersQuery}`;
    return `/api/v1/evaluation/batch?${featureFlagEvaluationQuery}`;
}
  function getAnalyticsPlatform(userAgent) {
    switch(true){
        case /windows phone/i.test(userAgent):
            return 'web_unknown';
        case /iPad/.test(userAgent):
            return 'web_desktop';
        case /android/i.test(userAgent) && /mobile/i.test(userAgent):
            return 'web_android';
        case /iPhone/.test(userAgent):
            return 'web_ios';
        default:
            return 'web_desktop';
    }
}
  function withRetries(f, retries) {
    return retries > 0 ? f().catch(()=>withRetries(f, retries - 1)) : f();
}
  function runScript(flagrUrl, flagrServerCtx) {
    window.auidCookie = auidCookie;
    const maybeCurrentAuid = auidCookie();
    window.auid = maybeCurrentAuid ? (fetch("/auid/refresh", {
        priority: "low"
    }), Promise.resolve(maybeCurrentAuid)) : withRetries(()=>fetch("/auid/refresh", {
            priority: "high"
        }).then((res)=>res.ok ? auidCookie() : Promise.reject(new Error(`Auid service responded with ${res.status}`))), 2);
    window.clientFlagrContext = window.auid.catch(()=>null).then((maybeAuid)=>({
            ...flagrServerCtx,
            auid: maybeAuid,
            web_client: getAnalyticsPlatform(navigator.userAgent)
        })).then((clientFlagsCtx)=>({
            clientFlagsCtx,
            flagrRequestUrl: flagrUrl + clientFlagrRequestUri(clientFlagsCtx)
        }));
    window.clientFlags = window.clientFlagrContext.then(({ flagrRequestUrl })=>withRetries(()=>fetch(flagrRequestUrl, {
                priority: "high"
            }).then((res)=>res.ok ? res.json() : Promise.reject(new Error(`Flagr responded with ${res.status}`))), 2));
}
  runScript("https://flagr.aviasales.com", {"brand":"AS","environment":"production","lang":"en","market":"us","platform":"web"})
} catch (e) { window.headScriptCrash = e }
</script>

            <script>
window.__ALLOW_DARK_THEME__ = true;
window.initTheme = function initTheme(theme) {
    var root = document.documentElement;
    var isTouchDevice = false;
    var targetTheme = 'light';
    var savedTheme = '';
    try {
        isTouchDevice = window.matchMedia('(hover: none)').matches;
        if (isTouchDevice) {
            root.classList.add('--is-touch-device');
        }
    } catch (_e) {
    // ok
    }
    try {
        if (!theme) {
            savedTheme = localStorage.getItem('userTheme');
            if (savedTheme) {
                targetTheme = savedTheme;
            }
        } else {
            targetTheme = theme;
        }
        if (window.__ALLOW_DARK_THEME__ === false && targetTheme === 'dark') {
            targetTheme = 'light';
        }
        if (targetTheme === 'dark') {
            if (!root.classList.contains('--night')) {
                root.classList.add('--night');
            }
        } else {
            if (root.classList.contains('--night')) {
                root.classList.remove('--night');
            }
        }
    } catch (err) {
        console.error(new Error('Failed to init saved theme', {
            cause: err
        }));
    }
};
window.initTheme();
</script>
